    git-svn-id: https://despotify.svn.sourceforge.net/svnroot/despotify@378 bd1f9101-17e2-4937-9e80-6147bc4d7589
    0.4.5
    
    Response unmarshalling using JDK 1.6 XML stream, although only supported by LoadArtist and LoadAlbum so far. Have seen speeds 5x-20x faster than the previous DOM parser. The bottleneck now is retrieving and gunzipping data.
    
    The unmarshalling is failfast, if an new tag is added to the response it needs to be handled in the code or it will throw an exception. This should be turned on and off using a setting in the future.
    
    Of course this feature made that I found all this new data in the response. similar albums, reviews, external ids, and what not. Some of this data is skipped (especially links) but most of it is added to the domain objects.
    
    Some data is shared by many classes but not extended from a single class. Need to think that though I think RestrictedMedia should be renamed to something else and also include links, external ids, et c.
    
    The XML schemas should be up to date with the data I've encountred, they do however need to be cleaned up.

    git-svn-id: https://despotify.svn.sourceforge.net/svnroot/despotify@346 bd1f9101-17e2-4937-9e80-6147bc4d7589
    Inital import of Java client
    
    
    git-svn-id: https://despotify.svn.sourceforge.net/svnroot/despotify@305 bd1f9101-17e2-4937-9e80-6147bc4d7589
    git-svn-id: https://despotify.svn.sourceforge.net/svnroot/despotify@378 bd1f9101-17e2-4937-9e80-6147bc4d7589
    0.4.5
    
    Response unmarshalling using JDK 1.6 XML stream, although only supported by LoadArtist and LoadAlbum so far. Have seen speeds 5x-20x faster than the previous DOM parser. The bottleneck now is retrieving and gunzipping data.
    
    The unmarshalling is failfast, if an new tag is added to the response it needs to be handled in the code or it will throw an exception. This should be turned on and off using a setting in the future.
    
    Of course this feature made that I found all this new data in the response. similar albums, reviews, external ids, and what not. Some of this data is skipped (especially links) but most of it is added to the domain objects.
    
    Some data is shared by many classes but not extended from a single class. Need to think that though I think RestrictedMedia should be renamed to something else and also include links, external ids, et c.
    
    The XML schemas should be up to date with the data I've encountred, they do however need to be cleaned up.

    Inital import of Java client
    
    
    git-svn-id: https://despotify.svn.sourceforge.net/svnroot/despotify@305 bd1f9101-17e2-4937-9e80-6147bc4d7589
    git-svn-id: https://despotify.svn.sourceforge.net/svnroot/despotify@378 bd1f9101-17e2-4937-9e80-6147bc4d7589
    0.4.5
    
    Response unmarshalling using JDK 1.6 XML stream, although only supported by LoadArtist and LoadAlbum so far. Have seen speeds 5x-20x faster than the previous DOM parser. The bottleneck now is retrieving and gunzipping data.
    
    The unmarshalling is failfast, if an new tag is added to the response it needs to be handled in the code or it will throw an exception. This should be turned on and off using a setting in the future.
    
    Of course this feature made that I found all this new data in the response. similar albums, reviews, external ids, and what not. Some of this data is skipped (especially links) but most of it is added to the domain objects.
    
    Some data is shared by many classes but not extended from a single class. Need to think that though I think RestrictedMedia should be renamed to something else and also include links, external ids, et c.
    
    The XML schemas should be up to date with the data I've encountred, they do however need to be cleaned up.

    Inital import of Java client
    
    
    git-svn-id: https://despotify.svn.sourceforge.net/svnroot/despotify@305 bd1f9101-17e2-4937-9e80-6147bc4d7589
    git-svn-id: https://despotify.svn.sourceforge.net/svnroot/despotify@378 bd1f9101-17e2-4937-9e80-6147bc4d7589
    0.4.5
    
    Response unmarshalling using JDK 1.6 XML stream, although only supported by LoadArtist and LoadAlbum so far. Have seen speeds 5x-20x faster than the previous DOM parser. The bottleneck now is retrieving and gunzipping data.
    
    The unmarshalling is failfast, if an new tag is added to the response it needs to be handled in the code or it will throw an exception. This should be turned on and off using a setting in the future.
    
    Of course this feature made that I found all this new data in the response. similar albums, reviews, external ids, and what not. Some of this data is skipped (especially links) but most of it is added to the domain objects.
    
    Some data is shared by many classes but not extended from a single class. Need to think that though I think RestrictedMedia should be renamed to something else and also include links, external ids, et c.
    
    The XML schemas should be up to date with the data I've encountred, they do however need to be cleaned up.

    git-svn-id: https://despotify.svn.sourceforge.net/svnroot/despotify@370 bd1f9101-17e2-4937-9e80-6147bc4d7589
    git-svn-id: https://despotify.svn.sourceforge.net/svnroot/despotify@378 bd1f9101-17e2-4937-9e80-6147bc4d7589
    0.4.5
    
    Response unmarshalling using JDK 1.6 XML stream, although only supported by LoadArtist and LoadAlbum so far. Have seen speeds 5x-20x faster than the previous DOM parser. The bottleneck now is retrieving and gunzipping data.
    
    The unmarshalling is failfast, if an new tag is added to the response it needs to be handled in the code or it will throw an exception. This should be turned on and off using a setting in the future.
    
    Of course this feature made that I found all this new data in the response. similar albums, reviews, external ids, and what not. Some of this data is skipped (especially links) but most of it is added to the domain objects.
    
    Some data is shared by many classes but not extended from a single class. Need to think that though I think RestrictedMedia should be renamed to something else and also include links, external ids, et c.
    
    The XML schemas should be up to date with the data I've encountred, they do however need to be cleaned up.

    git-svn-id: https://despotify.svn.sourceforge.net/svnroot/despotify@368 bd1f9101-17e2-4937-9e80-6147bc4d7589
    Support for newly discovered <track><similar-tracks/></track>
    Uncertain if only available on LoadTracks, i.e. perhaps not on LoadArtist, LoadAlbum or Search.
    
    See track cf1a5e24d32340499c611e2868bc05c1 for example:
    
        <track>
          <id>cf1a5e24d32340499c611e2868bc05c1</id>
          <title>Don&apos;t Think Twice It&apos;s All Right</title>
          <artist-id>f748ac6d66c545b1aeda1f6c97d7ebb0</artist-id>
          <artist>Waylon Jennings</artist>
          <album>Now! Country For Old Men</album>
          <album-id>b422bd31232742edb5191dc952e98b8d</album-id>
          <year>2008</year>
          <track-number>3</track-number>
          <length>161907</length>
          <files>
            <file id="af54f6408b2ebdcb6fa9b5e547f110a92a2cc25a" format="Ogg Vorbis,160000,1,32,4" /></files>
          <cover>dec895a650fe5f743ff6ace440d7d7ca6068631b</cover>
          <popularity>0.56204</popularity>
          <restrictions>
            <restriction forbidden="BL,ME,MF,RS,ZZ" catalogues="free,daypass,premium" />
          </restrictions>
          <forbidden>BL ME MF RS ZZ</forbidden>
          <similar-tracks>
            <id>c3245d6611de4ea6898f50c80f1dc33b</id>
            <id>31d1e4ecbe124f349033338787523fc4</id>
            <id>68f7649c9d4b45dd8dd2ee7d741f86a6</id>
            <id>34a6dcc391b045e387632cdab2423856</id>
            <id>38622498d2ac4631a4c7a16fd5c483af</id>
            <id>4e1f0ebcdd1f4382babde803cb75a508</id>
            <id>308cad6470b544efb4ee609696274a33</id>
            <id>7d2cb96ed4984ed885101947d51d9e21</id>
            <id>5c73809784b04b3aad69d0aa342279b5</id>

    git-svn-id: https://despotify.svn.sourceforge.net/svnroot/despotify@305 bd1f9101-17e2-4937-9e80-6147bc4d7589
    git-svn-id: https://despotify.svn.sourceforge.net/svnroot/despotify@378 bd1f9101-17e2-4937-9e80-6147bc4d7589
    0.4.5
    
    Response unmarshalling using JDK 1.6 XML stream, although only supported by LoadArtist and LoadAlbum so far. Have seen speeds 5x-20x faster than the previous DOM parser. The bottleneck now is retrieving and gunzipping data.
    
    The unmarshalling is failfast, if an new tag is added to the response it needs to be handled in the code or it will throw an exception. This should be turned on and off using a setting in the future.
    
    Of course this feature made that I found all this new data in the response. similar albums, reviews, external ids, and what not. Some of this data is skipped (especially links) but most of it is added to the domain objects.
    
    Some data is shared by many classes but not extended from a single class. Need to think that though I think RestrictedMedia should be renamed to something else and also include links, external ids, et c.
    
    The XML schemas should be up to date with the data I've encountred, they do however need to be cleaned up.

    git-svn-id: https://despotify.svn.sourceforge.net/svnroot/despotify@378 bd1f9101-17e2-4937-9e80-6147bc4d7589
    0.4.5
    
    Response unmarshalling using JDK 1.6 XML stream, although only supported by LoadArtist and LoadAlbum so far. Have seen speeds 5x-20x faster than the previous DOM parser. The bottleneck now is retrieving and gunzipping data.
    
    The unmarshalling is failfast, if an new tag is added to the response it needs to be handled in the code or it will throw an exception. This should be turned on and off using a setting in the future.
    
    Of course this feature made that I found all this new data in the response. similar albums, reviews, external ids, and what not. Some of this data is skipped (especially links) but most of it is added to the domain objects.
    
    Some data is shared by many classes but not extended from a single class. Need to think that though I think RestrictedMedia should be renamed to something else and also include links, external ids, et c.
    
    The XML schemas should be up to date with the data I've encountred, they do however need to be cleaned up.

    git-svn-id: https://despotify.svn.sourceforge.net/svnroot/despotify@386 bd1f9101-17e2-4937-9e80-6147bc4d7589

    git-svn-id: https://despotify.svn.sourceforge.net/svnroot/despotify@380 bd1f9101-17e2-4937-9e80-6147bc4d7589
    0.4.5
    
    Response unmarshalling using JDK 1.6 XML stream, although only supported by LoadArtist and LoadAlbum so far. Have seen speeds 5x-20x faster than the previous DOM parser. The bottleneck now is retrieving and gunzipping data.
    
    The unmarshalling is failfast, if an new tag is added to the response it needs to be handled in the code or it will throw an exception. This should be turned on and off using a setting in the future.
    
    Of course this feature made that I found all this new data in the response. similar albums, reviews, external ids, and what not. Some of this data is skipped (especially links) but most of it is added to the domain objects.
    
    Some data is shared by many classes but not extended from a single class. Need to think that though I think RestrictedMedia should be renamed to something else and also include links, external ids, et c.
    
    The XML schemas should be up to date with the data I've encountred, they do however need to be cleaned up.

    git-svn-id: https://despotify.svn.sourceforge.net/svnroot/despotify@384 bd1f9101-17e2-4937-9e80-6147bc4d7589
    0.4.5
    
    Response unmarshalling using JDK 1.6 XML stream, although only supported by LoadArtist and LoadAlbum so far. Have seen speeds 5x-20x faster than the previous DOM parser. The bottleneck now is retrieving and gunzipping data.
    
    The unmarshalling is failfast, if an new tag is added to the response it needs to be handled in the code or it will throw an exception. This should be turned on and off using a setting in the future.
    
    Of course this feature made that I found all this new data in the response. similar albums, reviews, external ids, and what not. Some of this data is skipped (especially links) but most of it is added to the domain objects.
    
    Some data is shared by many classes but not extended from a single class. Need to think that though I think RestrictedMedia should be renamed to something else and also include links, external ids, et c.
    
    The XML schemas should be up to date with the data I've encountred, they do however need to be cleaned up.

    git-svn-id: https://despotify.svn.sourceforge.net/svnroot/despotify@307 bd1f9101-17e2-4937-9e80-6147bc4d7589
    0.4.5
    
    Response unmarshalling using JDK 1.6 XML stream, although only supported by LoadArtist and LoadAlbum so far. Have seen speeds 5x-20x faster than the previous DOM parser. The bottleneck now is retrieving and gunzipping data.
    
    The unmarshalling is failfast, if an new tag is added to the response it needs to be handled in the code or it will throw an exception. This should be turned on and off using a setting in the future.
    
    Of course this feature made that I found all this new data in the response. similar albums, reviews, external ids, and what not. Some of this data is skipped (especially links) but most of it is added to the domain objects.
    
    Some data is shared by many classes but not extended from a single class. Need to think that though I think RestrictedMedia should be renamed to something else and also include links, external ids, et c.
    
    The XML schemas should be up to date with the data I've encountred, they do however need to be cleaned up.

    git-svn-id: https://despotify.svn.sourceforge.net/svnroot/despotify@342 bd1f9101-17e2-4937-9e80-6147bc4d7589
    0.4.5
    
    Response unmarshalling using JDK 1.6 XML stream, although only supported by LoadArtist and LoadAlbum so far. Have seen speeds 5x-20x faster than the previous DOM parser. The bottleneck now is retrieving and gunzipping data.
    
    The unmarshalling is failfast, if an new tag is added to the response it needs to be handled in the code or it will throw an exception. This should be turned on and off using a setting in the future.
    
    Of course this feature made that I found all this new data in the response. similar albums, reviews, external ids, and what not. Some of this data is skipped (especially links) but most of it is added to the domain objects.
    
    Some data is shared by many classes but not extended from a single class. Need to think that though I think RestrictedMedia should be renamed to something else and also include links, external ids, et c.
    
    The XML schemas should be up to date with the data I've encountred, they do however need to be cleaned up.
    
    
    git-svn-id: https://despotify.svn.sourceforge.net/svnroot/despotify@377 bd1f9101-17e2-4937-9e80-6147bc4d7589

    git-svn-id: https://despotify.svn.sourceforge.net/svnroot/despotify@377 bd1f9101-17e2-4937-9e80-6147bc4d7589
    0.4.5
    
    Response unmarshalling using JDK 1.6 XML stream, although only supported by LoadArtist and LoadAlbum so far. Have seen speeds 5x-20x faster than the previous DOM parser. The bottleneck now is retrieving and gunzipping data.
    
    The unmarshalling is failfast, if an new tag is added to the response it needs to be handled in the code or it will throw an exception. This should be turned on and off using a setting in the future.
    
    Of course this feature made that I found all this new data in the response. similar albums, reviews, external ids, and what not. Some of this data is skipped (especially links) but most of it is added to the domain objects.
    
    Some data is shared by many classes but not extended from a single class. Need to think that though I think RestrictedMedia should be renamed to something else and also include links, external ids, et c.
    
    The XML schemas should be up to date with the data I've encountred, they do however need to be cleaned up.

    git-svn-id: https://despotify.svn.sourceforge.net/svnroot/despotify@381 bd1f9101-17e2-4937-9e80-6147bc4d7589
    mostly JPA and XML response unmarshalling related fixes.
    
    git-svn-id: https://despotify.svn.sourceforge.net/svnroot/despotify@380 bd1f9101-17e2-4937-9e80-6147bc4d7589
    0.4.5
    
    Response unmarshalling using JDK 1.6 XML stream, although only supported by LoadArtist and LoadAlbum so far. Have seen speeds 5x-20x faster than the previous DOM parser. The bottleneck now is retrieving and gunzipping data.
    
    The unmarshalling is failfast, if an new tag is added to the response it needs to be handled in the code or it will throw an exception. This should be turned on and off using a setting in the future.
    
    Of course this feature made that I found all this new data in the response. similar albums, reviews, external ids, and what not. Some of this data is skipped (especially links) but most of it is added to the domain objects.
    
    Some data is shared by many classes but not extended from a single class. Need to think that though I think RestrictedMedia should be renamed to something else and also include links, external ids, et c.
    
    The XML schemas should be up to date with the data I've encountred, they do however need to be cleaned up.
    
    
    git-svn-id: https://despotify.svn.sourceforge.net/svnroot/despotify@377 bd1f9101-17e2-4937-9e80-6147bc4d7589

    0.4.5
    
    Response unmarshalling using JDK 1.6 XML stream, although only supported by LoadArtist and LoadAlbum so far. Have seen speeds 5x-20x faster than the previous DOM parser. The bottleneck now is retrieving and gunzipping data.
    
    The unmarshalling is failfast, if an new tag is added to the response it needs to be handled in the code or it will throw an exception. This should be turned on and off using a setting in the future.
    
    Of course this feature made that I found all this new data in the response. similar albums, reviews, external ids, and what not. Some of this data is skipped (especially links) but most of it is added to the domain objects.
    
    Some data is shared by many classes but not extended from a single class. Need to think that though I think RestrictedMedia should be renamed to something else and also include links, external ids, et c.
    
    The XML schemas should be up to date with the data I've encountred, they do however need to be cleaned up.

    git-svn-id: https://despotify.svn.sourceforge.net/svnroot/despotify@384 bd1f9101-17e2-4937-9e80-6147bc4d7589
    0.4.5
    
    Response unmarshalling using JDK 1.6 XML stream, although only supported by LoadArtist and LoadAlbum so far. Have seen speeds 5x-20x faster than the previous DOM parser. The bottleneck now is retrieving and gunzipping data.
    
    The unmarshalling is failfast, if an new tag is added to the response it needs to be handled in the code or it will throw an exception. This should be turned on and off using a setting in the future.
    
    Of course this feature made that I found all this new data in the response. similar albums, reviews, external ids, and what not. Some of this data is skipped (especially links) but most of it is added to the domain objects.
    
    Some data is shared by many classes but not extended from a single class. Need to think that though I think RestrictedMedia should be renamed to something else and also include links, external ids, et c.
    
    The XML schemas should be up to date with the data I've encountred, they do however need to be cleaned up.

    git-svn-id: https://despotify.svn.sourceforge.net/svnroot/despotify@305 bd1f9101-17e2-4937-9e80-6147bc4d7589
    0.4.6
    
    git-svn-id: https://despotify.svn.sourceforge.net/svnroot/despotify@386 bd1f9101-17e2-4937-9e80-6147bc4d7589
    0.4.5
    
    Response unmarshalling using JDK 1.6 XML stream, although only supported by LoadArtist and LoadAlbum so far. Have seen speeds 5x-20x faster than the previous DOM parser. The bottleneck now is retrieving and gunzipping data.
    
    The unmarshalling is failfast, if an new tag is added to the response it needs to be handled in the code or it will throw an exception. This should be turned on and off using a setting in the future.
    
    Of course this feature made that I found all this new data in the response. similar albums, reviews, external ids, and what not. Some of this data is skipped (especially links) but most of it is added to the domain objects.
    
    Some data is shared by many classes but not extended from a single class. Need to think that though I think RestrictedMedia should be renamed to something else and also include links, external ids, et c.
    
    The XML schemas should be up to date with the data I've encountred, they do however need to be cleaned up.

    git-svn-id: https://despotify.svn.sourceforge.net/svnroot/despotify@387 bd1f9101-17e2-4937-9e80-6147bc4d7589
    0.4.6
    
    git-svn-id: https://despotify.svn.sourceforge.net/svnroot/despotify@386 bd1f9101-17e2-4937-9e80-6147bc4d7589
    0.4.5
    
    Response unmarshalling using JDK 1.6 XML stream, although only supported by LoadArtist and LoadAlbum so far. Have seen speeds 5x-20x faster than the previous DOM parser. The bottleneck now is retrieving and gunzipping data.
    
    The unmarshalling is failfast, if an new tag is added to the response it needs to be handled in the code or it will throw an exception. This should be turned on and off using a setting in the future.
    
    Of course this feature made that I found all this new data in the response. similar albums, reviews, external ids, and what not. Some of this data is skipped (especially links) but most of it is added to the domain objects.
    
    Some data is shared by many classes but not extended from a single class. Need to think that though I think RestrictedMedia should be renamed to something else and also include links, external ids, et c.
    
    The XML schemas should be up to date with the data I've encountred, they do however need to be cleaned up.

    git-svn-id: https://despotify.svn.sourceforge.net/svnroot/despotify@368 bd1f9101-17e2-4937-9e80-6147bc4d7589
    Support for newly discovered <track><similar-tracks/></track>
    Uncertain if only available on LoadTracks, i.e. perhaps not on LoadArtist, LoadAlbum or Search.
    
    See track cf1a5e24d32340499c611e2868bc05c1 for example:
    
        <track>
          <id>cf1a5e24d32340499c611e2868bc05c1</id>
          <title>Don&apos;t Think Twice It&apos;s All Right</title>
          <artist-id>f748ac6d66c545b1aeda1f6c97d7ebb0</artist-id>
          <artist>Waylon Jennings</artist>
          <album>Now! Country For Old Men</album>
          <album-id>b422bd31232742edb5191dc952e98b8d</album-id>
          <year>2008</year>
          <track-number>3</track-number>
          <length>161907</length>
          <files>
            <file id="af54f6408b2ebdcb6fa9b5e547f110a92a2cc25a" format="Ogg Vorbis,160000,1,32,4" /></files>
          <cover>dec895a650fe5f743ff6ace440d7d7ca6068631b</cover>
          <popularity>0.56204</popularity>
          <restrictions>
            <restriction forbidden="BL,ME,MF,RS,ZZ" catalogues="free,daypass,premium" />
          </restrictions>
          <forbidden>BL ME MF RS ZZ</forbidden>
          <similar-tracks>
            <id>c3245d6611de4ea6898f50c80f1dc33b</id>
            <id>31d1e4ecbe124f349033338787523fc4</id>
            <id>68f7649c9d4b45dd8dd2ee7d741f86a6</id>
            <id>34a6dcc391b045e387632cdab2423856</id>
            <id>38622498d2ac4631a4c7a16fd5c483af</id>
            <id>4e1f0ebcdd1f4382babde803cb75a508</id>
            <id>308cad6470b544efb4ee609696274a33</id>
            <id>7d2cb96ed4984ed885101947d51d9e21</id>
            <id>5c73809784b04b3aad69d0aa342279b5</id>
            <id>8da5cac165ef4346940070391409c44e</id>
            <id>0cdb299e5f884804bee42eff261c1a91</id>
            <id>7fc1bff95afd47138c81f5fddde8f58c</id>
            <id>c06b9a7bc3ac49c887385a49c2d452ae</id>
            <id>e6aaeab2a4b645db8d249da55c7b7713</id>
            <id>304f8692669b47f6b8980c8809ed6be1</id>
          </similar-tracks>
        </track>

    mostly JPA and XML response unmarshalling related fixes.
    
    git-svn-id: https://despotify.svn.sourceforge.net/svnroot/despotify@380 bd1f9101-17e2-4937-9e80-6147bc4d7589
    0.4.5
    
    Response unmarshalling using JDK 1.6 XML stream, although only supported by LoadArtist and LoadAlbum so far. Have seen speeds 5x-20x faster than the previous DOM parser. The bottleneck now is retrieving and gunzipping data.
    
    The unmarshalling is failfast, if an new tag is added to the response it needs to be handled in the code or it will throw an exception. This should be turned on and off using a setting in the future.
    
    Of course this feature made that I found all this new data in the response. similar albums, reviews, external ids, and what not. Some of this data is skipped (especially links) but most of it is added to the domain objects.
    
    Some data is shared by many classes but not extended from a single class. Need to think that though I think RestrictedMedia should be renamed to something else and also include links, external ids, et c.
    
    The XML schemas should be up to date with the data I've encountred, they do however need to be cleaned up.
    
    
    git-svn-id: https://despotify.svn.sourceforge.net/svnroot/despotify@377 bd1f9101-17e2-4937-9e80-6147bc4d7589
    0.4.5-SNAPSHOT
    Minimzed connection blocking calls. Started using Apache commons pool rather than the ad hoc solution. Changes behaviour for all clients that use this API, sorry about that.

    0.4.5
    
    Response unmarshalling using JDK 1.6 XML stream, although only supported by LoadArtist and LoadAlbum so far. Have seen speeds 5x-20x faster than the previous DOM parser. The bottleneck now is retrieving and gunzipping data.
    
    The unmarshalling is failfast, if an new tag is added to the response it needs to be handled in the code or it will throw an exception. This should be turned on and off using a setting in the future.

    Some data is shared by many classes but not extended from a single class. Need to think that though I think RestrictedMedia should be renamed to something else and also include links, external ids, et c.
    
    The XML schemas should be up to date with the data I've encountred, they do however need to be cleaned up.
